## 🔧 Mock Data Replacement Strategy

### Immediate Actions (Critical/High)
1. **Review credential placeholders** - Replace with environment variables
2. **Remove hardcoded test data** - Move to test fixtures or configuration
3. **Replace demo content** - Use real or configurable content

### Medium Term Actions (Medium/Low)
1. **Standardize placeholder patterns** - Use consistent naming
2. **Create configuration templates** - Separate example configs from working configs
3. **Move test fixtures** - Relocate to appropriate test directories

## 💡 Recommendations
- **URGENT**: Fix production-unsafe files before deployment
- Review and address all high-risk files
- Create environment variable configuration system
- Implement mock data scanning in CI/CD pipeline
- Document placeholder replacement procedures
- Create development vs production configuration guides
